    INNER JOIN [Cinemas] AS [c] ON [m].[CinemaId] = [c].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Producers] AS [p] ON [m].[ProducerId] = [p].[Id]
    WHERE [m].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]

    SELECT [a].[MovieId], [a].[ActorId], [a0].[Id], [a0].[Bio], [a0].[FullName], [a0].[ProfilePictureURL]

) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
